04 Mar 2017 03:07:33 : Cipher, cala, Wertfuzzy77#0274, ```Index = {}

WHILE Parser.hasMore() DO:
    Document = Parser.nextDocument()
    WHILE Document.hasMore() DO:
        Term = Document.nextTerm()
        ID = Document.getID()
        IF Term in Index.keys():
            Index[Term] append ID
        ELSE:
            Index[Term] = ID
        END IF
    END WHILE
END WHILE```

04 Mar 2017 03:13:54 : The Wild Weebs, general, enragednuke#2565, ```
function TAAT(term)
  pages = Index.getInvertedList(term)
  // Calculate every page's score for a given term, all at once (instead of every term for a given page at once)
  for each page in pages
    TF = iterate over page and increment when 'term' is found, store in variable
    TDF = calculate length of 'pages' variable above, store in variable
    TCF = iterate over all other pages in 'pages' variable, increment when 'term' is found, add to TF, store in variable
    Set page's search score for query term equal to Model.score(TF, TCF, TDF)
  endfor
endfunction
```
